 in Referring to the strong performance of the Indian economy even in challenging global conditions, President Pranab Mukherjee today said that it has the potential to become a $ 10,000 billion economy in the next two decades
 raashtrapati ne pragati maidan main 35wein bhartiya antarrashtriya vyapaar mela - 2015 (iitief) kaa udghaatan karte hue kaha ki gharelu str par ‘mek in india’ abhiyaan ke saath saath vinirmaan par jor die jane kii jarurat he
 He said that with this, the challenge arising from the external environment can be met by focusing on new export markets in Asia, Africa and Latin American countries
 pranab ne kaha, ham aaj 2,100 arab dollar kii arthvyavastha hai or yadi vinirmaan or navapravartan ko protsaahan diya jaataa he to agle do dashak main ham 10 hajaar arab dollar kii arthvyavastha ban sakate hai
 "our economy has been able to meet the challenging global economic scenario created during the last few years," he said
 duniya kii kai pramukh arthvyavasthaaon main chai aarthik susti se bharat kaaphi had tak bachaa rahaa
 The President said that except for the year 2012-13 when the economic growth had gone below five percent, the Indian economy has shown its strength continuously
 unhone kaha ki iske baad 2014-15 main 7
 After achieving 2 percent growth, the country's economy again started on the path of acceleration
 tippaniyan He said, it is expected to improve further as other macroeconomic indicators are showing considerable improvement

 Utpal Dutt, who won the hearts of the audience with his performance in the film Golmaal (1979)
 unka janm 29 march, 1929 ko purvi bengal (british bharat) ke barisal main ek hindu parivaar main hua tha
 His father's name was Girijaranjan Dutt
 utpal ne 1945 main metric kii pariksha paas kii or 1949 main saint jevier college, kolkata se angreji sahitya main snaatak kii degree praapt kii
 Utpal Dutt started his acting career in 1940 by joining English theater
 unhen shakespeare sahitya se behad lagaav tha
 During this time he staged many plays with theater company not only in India but also in Pakistan
 naatak othelo ke liye unhen kaaphi prashansa mili thi
 Later Utpal moved from English to Bengali drama
 1950 ke baad unhone ek production company join kar lee or yahaan se unhone bengali filmon ke liye kaam karnaa shuru kar diya
 During this time he did not leave the theater
 unhone kai naatakon ko nirdesan hi nahin balki lekhan kaary bhi kiya
 He wrote many plays on Bengali politics that gave rise to controversies
 utpal dutt acting ke saath-saath naatak likhane ke bhi shaukeen the
 Many of his plays drew on the political conditions of the time
 kai naatak vivaadon main rahe
 The political parties of that time used to be very disturbed by the plays written by Utpal
 isliye jab bhi utpal kuch likhane kii taiyaariyaan shuru karte the to partiyaan pehle hi unhen rokane ke intjaam karnaa shuru kar detii thim
 Utpal was heavily influenced by the leftist ideology
 ve vampanthi dalon ke liye naatak likhaa karte the
 His plays used to be on such a subject that the government began to doubt his patriotism
 us dauraan unhen angaar or kallor naatak likhane par bina kisi trial ke jail bhej diya gaya tha
 Utpal Dutt died on 19 August 1993
 unhone lagbhag 100 se zyada filmon main kaam kiya tha

 yani aarakshak umesh sharma ab apane puure sarvice kaal tak milane vaali selary main se har saal ek maheene kii selary sena welfare fund main denge
